### 1. 高速微距美食摄影：酸奶中的奇异果切片

**Author**: [𝐌](https://x.com/Strength04_X)  **Date**: 2026-02-09  **Language**: en

> 一个结构化提示，用于生成一张超现实、高速的微距照片，内容为一片新鲜的奇异果切片悬浮在半空中，被一股柔滑的淡绿色奇异果酸奶轻轻包裹，强调干净的商业美学、超高细节和纯白色背景。

```
{
  "image_type": "photograph",
  "genre": "high-speed macro food photography",
  "subject": {
    "main_object": "fresh {argument name="fruit type" default="kiwi"} slice",
    "state": "suspended mid-air",
    "interaction": "softly wrapped by a gentle flow of pale {argument name="yogurt flavor" default="green kiwi"} yogurt"
  },
  "composition": {
    "framing": "tight macro close-up",
    "orientation": "vertical",
    "subject_position": "centered",
    "isolation": "isolated object, clean cutout"
  },
  "motion": {
    "liquid_behavior": "smooth, restrained liquid motion",
    "splash_intensity": "minimal splash",
    "droplets": "very few small droplets",
    "fluid_dynamics": "calm and controlled"
  },
  "texture_and_detail": {
    "yogurt_texture": "thick, creamy, silky",
    "fruit_texture": "ultra-realistic kiwi flesh with visible seeds",
    "surface_detail": "high micro-detail, natural moisture"
  },
  "lighting": {
    "style": "professional studio lighting",
    "highlights": "soft diffuse highlights",
    "shadows": "gentle, natural falloff",
    "exposure": "balanced, high dynamic range"
  },
  "background": {
    "color": "pure white",
    "style": "seamless studio backdrop"
  },
  "quality": {
    "realism": "photorealistic",
    "resolution": "ultra-high resolution",
    "sharpness": "crisp focus on subject"
  },
  "constraints": [
    "no CGI",
    "no 3D render",
    "no illustration",
    "no artificial look"
  ],
  "aesthetic": "clean, premium, commercial food advertising style"
}
```

### 3. 超逼真微缩蒸汽朋克栖息地立体模型

**Author**: [Artingent](https://x.com/artingent)  **Date**: 2026-02-03  **Language**: en

> 一个高度受限的提示，用于生成一个微型蒸汽朋克栖息地的超现实微距照片，该栖息地建造在一个金属橱柜内部，严格执行比例一致性和真实的相机行为，适用于立体模型可视化。

```
[VARIABLE – Habitat Type]: {argument name="habitat type" default="Steampunk"}

[VARIABLE – Scale]:
Miniature humans approximately 1:300 relative to the metallic cupboard. All humans, animals, tools, furniture, machinery, pipes, gears, steam systems, lighting elements, architectural details, and clothing strictly follow this exact same scale, with absolutely no variation or mixed sizing. No mixed scale, no inconsistent proportions, no oversized figures, no undersized figures, no giant humans, no micro-humans, no toy-scale artifacts, no dollhouse proportions, no caricature anatomy, no stylized exaggeration, no chibi forms, no abstract scaling, and no perspective cheats. Every human figure is consistently proportioned to one another, to their attire, and to the cupboard environment, physically plausible and usable at that scale.

[VARIABLE – Camera Framing]:
Hyper-realistic miniature macro photography, diorama-style cutaway view, wide framing that captures the entire metallic cupboard while clearly revealing all interior shelves, compartments, and structural divisions. No cropped subject, no partial furniture, no forced close-ups, no extreme fisheye distortion, no warped geometry, no impossible camera angles, no orthographic flattening, and no illustration-style framing. Shallow depth of field is present but never obscures scale clarity, with realistic lens behavior and museum-quality miniature realism.

[VARIABLE – External Setting]:
An indoor room environment at full real-world scale, such as a kitchen, workshop, or utility space, with subtle background elements like walls, floor, ambient indoor lighting, and surrounding objects kept soft and unobtrusive. No oversized humans, no hands interacting with the cupboard, no modern branding emphasis, no text labels, no product-shot staging, and no unrealistic studio backdrops.

[VARIABLE – Time of Day / Weather]:
Indoor daytime lighting with soft, neutral ambient illumination and gentle directional highlights. No dramatic cinematic lighting, no nighttime mood lighting, no sunset coloration, no harsh spotlights, no exaggerated reflections, and no color grading that overrides physical realism.

[Subject]:
A fully visible metallic cupboard shown as a clean, intentional cutaway cross-section, transformed into a complete {argument name="habitat type" default="Steampunk"} miniature human habitat. The cupboard exists at normal, real-world proportions within its external setting, appearing as an ordinary storage unit. No fantasy furniture shapes, no futuristic materials, no oversized handles, no pristine showroom condition, and no floating or levitating positioning. Inside the cupboard, all miniature human beings are rendered at the exact same scale defined in the Scale variable, with no oversized or undersized figures and no scale drift between compartments. The tiny inhabitants go about their daily lives—operating steam valves, maintaining brass machinery, forgi
```

[[Macro Photography]] [[Steampunk Aesthetic]]

### 28. 苏打水罐的宏观产品特写

### 29. 有缺陷发明的历史档案员提示

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2025-12-30  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的多阶段提示，旨在让 AI 扮演历史档案管理员的角色，生成一张照片级的微距照片，展示一个容器，其中装满了用户指定时代中四个鲜为人知、失败的历史原型实物，并配有清晰可辨的手写标签，详细说明了该发明及其致命缺陷。

![有缺陷发明的历史档案员提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767454930384_i85347_G9TrT6_WQAE5a3t.jpg)
![有缺陷发明的历史档案员提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767454930718_xcrera_G9Trm2aXIAAcNTP.jpg)

```
Role: Historical Archivist & Technical Illustrator.
Input Era/Region: {argument name="era and region" default="US, 1820s"}

Phase 1: The Deep Dive (AI to Deduce)
1.  Identify Container: Era-appropriate storage (Chest, Cabinet, Box).
2.  Identify Paperwork: Era-appropriate medium (Vellum, Blueprints, Floppy Disks).
3.  Identify 4 Obscure Failures:
    Constraint: Do NOT select famous successes. Select Bizarre, Failed, or Dangerous prototypes.
   Data Extraction: For each item, identify its Historical Name and its Fatal Flaw.

Phase 2: The Visual Translation Layer (Geometry)
Logic: The AI must explicitly analyze the Physical Form Factor of each selected invention.
Instruction: Do not render generic shapes. If it's a "Steam Man," render a brass robot. If it's a "Pneumatic Tube," render the piping.

Phase 3: Visual Execution
Subject: The [Container] overflowing with the [Signature Geometries] of the lost inventions.

1. The "Lost" Prototypes:
Render the 4 inventions based strictly on their Physical Form Factor.
Material: Authentic materials (Brass, Wood, Bakelite, Clay) based on the era.

2. The Labels (CRITICAL UPDATE):
Format: Each item has a clearly attached tag (String/Wax/Adhesive) with Legible Text.
Text Structure:
Line 1:[The Invention Name] (e.g., "The Dynasphere").
Line 2:[The Flaw] (e.g., "Unstable Steering").
Note:Ensure the text looks handwritten or stamped according to the time period.

3. The Narrative:
The Inventors: Tiny figurines reacting to the failure (frustrated, crying, kicking the machine).
The Contrast: A generic Modern Smartphone (or futuristic device) sitting on the edge for scale/irony.

4. Atmosphere:
Lighting: Dramatic, moody, specific to the era.
Texture: Macro details of rust, dust, and age.

Output: ONE image, 4:5, Photorealistic Macro Photography, Legible Text Labels.
```

### 30. 宏观透视模型：历史宿敌（科学战争）

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2025-12-29  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的多阶段提示，旨在生成一幅超详细的宏观立体模型图像，描绘历史或现代的竞争（例如，埃隆·马斯克与竞争对手）。它需要整合符合时代的文件（“舞台”）、穿着时代服装的微型对手人偶、巨大的工具，以及至关重要的是，清晰可辨的环境文本（身份锚点），以便在没有浮动文本的情况下标记人物。这个提示是高度概念化和结构化的。

![宏观透视模型：历史宿敌（科学战争）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767166866151_b0xdhd_G9B-1KFWIAAuVhM.jpg)
![宏观透视模型：历史宿敌（科学战争）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767166866879_kr768n_G9B-1KFXMAA8otj.jpg)

```
<instructions> 
Input: Invention/Rivalry = {argument name="invention/rivalry" default="[User Choice]"}

Phase 1: Chronological Profiling
Ancient (Pre-500 AD): Stone/Papyrus, Oil Lamps. Labeling = Carved symbols or scroll signatures.
Renaissance (1400-1600): Parchment, Candlelight. Labeling = Wax seals, hand-lettered envelopes, book spines.
Industrial (1800-1940): Blueprints, Gaslight. Labeling = Typed Patent headers, Business Cards, Newspaper Headlines.
Modern (1950-Present): Circuit diagrams, Neon. Labeling = ID Badges, Magazine covers, Computer login screens.

Phase 2:
Goal: A hyper-detailed Macro Diorama where the environment identifies the rivals.

1. The Stage (The Document):
 The ground is the primary design medium of the era (Clay Tablet, Parchment, Blueprint, or CAD Printout).
The Invention:A 3D Prototype is rising from the center, separating the two figures.

2. The Living Miniatures: Two tiny, hyper-realistic figurines (The Rivals) interact with the invention.
  They are dressed strictly in period-accurate clothing.

3. The Identity Anchors (CRITICAL - Labeling):
Instruction: You must seamlessly integrate readable text into the "Giant" props near each figure to identify them to the viewer.
Prop A (Near Rival 1): Place a "Giant" personal item with their name visible. (e.g., A letter addressed to "Mr. T. Edison", a book titled "By C. Darwin", or a security badge reading "S. Jobs").
Prop B (Near Rival 2):Do the same for the second figure. (e.g., A Patent application signed "Nikola Tesla", or a court summons for "Mark Zuckerberg").
Context: These items must look like they were carelessly left on the desk, not floating labels.

4. The "Giant" Atmosphere:
The Tools: Giant-scale era-appropriate tools (Chisels, Quills, Soldering Irons) tower over the figures.
The Clutter: Period-specific debris (Marble dust, Ink spills, Burnt fuses, Empty soda cans).

5. Technical Specs:
Lighting: Era-appropriate source (Fire vs. Filament vs. LED).
Perspective:Tilt-shift macro photography (45-degree angle). focus on the miniatures.

Output: ONE image, 4:5 aspect ratio, photorealistic historical macro photography with legible environmental text. </instructions>
```

### 35. 历史宏观立体透视模型：烹饪地图网格

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2025-12-27  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的多阶段提示，旨在根据用户选择的食材生成一个 2x2 的“历史宏观立体模型”网格。它要求 AI 首先确定一个“时代质感”（古代、文艺复兴、工业、现代），然后创建一张凌乱工作台的超细节微距照片。每个面板都展示了一本打开的书，其中包含 2D 草图和一个已完成餐点的 3D 弹出式立体模型，以及一个发明家和一个竞争对手的微型时代精确小雕像。

![历史宏观立体透视模型：烹饪地图网格](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766987648345_zwo194_G9B-BdaXoAAdW5M.jpg)
![历史宏观立体透视模型：烹饪地图网格](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766987648285_yidarh_G9B-BdSXAAAbtMq.jpg)

```
Role:Historical Art Director & Macro Photographer.
Input: Invention or Rivalry = [{argument name="user choice" default="User Choice"}]

Phase 1: Chronological Profiling
Before rendering, analyze the Year of the invention to determine the "Era Texture":
If Ancient (e.g., 200 BC): Surface = Rough Stone or Papyrus. Light = Oil Lamp/Torch. Clutter = Clay shards, bronze chisels, scrolls, figs/grapes.
If Renaissance (e.g., 1500): Surface = Dark Oak & Vellum. Light = Candle. Clutter = Quill feathers, wax seals, brass astrolabes, leather binding.
If Industrial (e.g., 1890): Surface = Green Felt or Mahogany. Light = Gas/Filament. Clutter = Newsprint, pocket watches, copper wire, soot.
If Modern (e.g., 1980): Surface = Formica or Metal. Light = Fluorescent/Neon. Clutter = Circuit boards, Polaroid photos, soda cans, plastic casings.

Phase 2: Visual Execution
Goal: A hyper-detailed "Macro Diorama" where the environment tells the story of the time period.
Subject: A messy, chaotic workspace viewed through a macro lens.

1. The Stage (The Document):
The "ground" is the primary design medium of that era 
The surface is filled with era-specific sketches/carvings of the invention.

2. The Living Miniatures:
Two tiny, hyper-realistic figurines (The Inventor & The Rival) stand on this surface.
They are dressed strictly in period-accurate clothing (Togas vs. Frock Coats vs. Turtlenecks).
Action: They are interacting with a 3D Prototype of the invention that is rising physically out of the document/tablet.

3. The "Giant" Atmosphere (Dynamic Enrichment):
The Wall: A massive background object establishing context (e.g., a carved stone stele, a tapestried wall, a vintage newspaper, or a stack of VHS tapes).
The Tools: Giant-scale tools used to make the invention loom over the figures like trees (e.g., a giant chisel, a massive quill dipped in ink, or a soldering iron).
The Debris: The mess of the creative process (e.g., stone dust, spilled ink, burnt fuses, or crumpled layout paper).
The Comforts: Food/Drink of the era (e.g., an earthen jug of wine, a porcelain tea cup, or a can of cola).

4. Technical Specs:
Lighting: Must match the "Era Light" determined in Phase 1 (Flickering warm fire vs. cold electric buzz).
Perspective: Tilt-shift macro photography (45-degree angle).
Texture: Extreme focus on material weathering (rust, dust, parchment cracks, or plastic sheen).

Output: ONE image, 4:5 aspect ratio, "Historical Macro Realism."
```

[[Macro Photography]] [[Miniature Diorama]] [[Grid Composition]]

**Author**: [Ray Zhai](https://x.com/Cryptoxorz)  **Date**: 2025-12-27  **Language**: zh

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 准备的详细提示词，最初基于一个“香蕉”提示词，但已通用化以适用于任何产品，专门用于生成两颗奢华樱桃的超写实微距摄影。该提示词包含照明（珠宝摄影）、构图和“黑钻石”主题的广告文案等技术细节。

![奢华樱桃产品摄影提示（黑钻）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766987762991_827nh5_G9Lrn40agAAIEio.jpg)

![奢华樱桃产品摄影提示（黑钻）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766987767581_9gsx9w_G9Lrn4ybMAAu97V.jpg)

```
主体： {argument name="subject" default="两颗深红得近乎发黑的顶级车厘子"}，紧挨在一起，果柄翠绿且相连。细节： 微距镜头下，果皮表面呈现出极其光滑、如镜面般的质感，清晰地反射出影棚的光源。一颗极小的、晶莹剔透的水珠停留在其中一颗果实的最圆润处，摇摇欲坠。光线： 精细的专业珠宝摄影布光。利用柔光箱创造出锐利而干净的长条形高光带，完美勾勒出果实的球体曲线和深邃的色泽。色彩： 深宝石红、墨黑、高光白、翠绿（果柄）。氛围： 极致诱惑、珍贵、奢华、令人垂涎。技术参数： 微距摄影，极浅景深（聚焦于水珠和高光），8K分辨率，极致锐利，--ar 4:5 --v 6.0[ 🖋️ 文案与排版 ]

主标题： {argument name="main title" default="黑 钻 (BLACK DIAMOND)"}
副标题： 32mm+ 仅供挑剔的味蕾。
底部文字： RARE & EXQUISITE
排版建议： 居中对齐。标题使用纤细高雅的衬线体，颜色为金色或白色。
```

### 42. 基于物体的微型超现实生态系统

**Author**: [Saul Goodman](https://x.com/Goodmanprotocol)  **Date**: 2025-12-18  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的提示，用于生成一个超详细、微型、超现实的世界，该世界完全围绕一个上传的物体构建。该提示要求微小、栩栩如生的人物与该物体互动，仿佛它就是他们的完整环境，并规定物体的几何形状（凹槽、螺丝、边缘）必须定义世界的建筑和地形。

![基于物体的微型超现实生态系统](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766237834583_blbplr_G8c0v3YakAol9wL.jpg)

```
Create an ultra-detailed, miniature, surreal world built entirely around the object shown in the uploaded image. Design tiny, lifelike figures that interact naturally and logically with the object as if it is their complete environment. Every element of architecture, terrain, tools, textures, and lighting must adapt organically to the object’s real physical form, materials, and surface characteristics.

Avoid any preconceived interpretations; instead, let the object’s geometry dictate the world’s design. Rails, optics, grooves, screws, edges, cavities, and mechanical components should naturally define pathways, platforms, work zones, and scale. The surrounding organic elements visible in the image should influence how the miniature world integrates with the object, creating a believable coexistence between natural textures and engineered surfaces.

Ensure the figures’ interactions feel grounded and observational, subtly emphasizing structure, material weight, and mechanical precision without dramatization, glorification, or promotion. The scene should feel physically plausible, quiet, and lived-in.

Render with photorealistic depth, cinematic macro photography, shallow depth of field, micro-details, soft volumetric lighting, and seamless integration between characters and the object. The final composition should feel like a believable, tiny ecosystem existing on and within the object itself.

Aspect ratio 16:9.
```

[[Macro Photography]] [[Surreal Photography]] [[Forced Perspective]] [[Miniature World]]

> 为 Nano Banana Pro 提供一个高度具体的提示，要求生成一张超写实的微距照片。照片内容为一位黑人女性在阵雨中使用一片巨大的三叶草叶子当伞，重点突出水滴、光亮的泥土以及阴沉多云的光线等复杂细节，并明确禁止生成小雕像或玩具。

Her face is damp with mist, wet strands of hair stick to her forehead, and the waterproof fabric of her coat shows realistic creases and water droplets. She is actively walking through a gentle rain shower, gripping the thick stem of a colossal, vibrant green clover leaf that she is using as an umbrella. The weight of the leaf strains her arm muscles slightly, and her boots sink into the wet, muddy soil. The scene is set on a damp forest floor, surrounded by giant pebbles and moss. The lighting is soft, overcast, and moody, highlighting the intricate veins of the leaf and the glossy wetness of the mud. The background is a heavily blurred macro bokeh of green foliage and falling rain.

### 68. 主题的微观视图

**Author**: [Stas Kulesh](https://x.com/stas_kulesh)  **Date**: 2025-12-10  **Language**: en

```
Ultra realistic 8K extreme close up face portrait of a young woman with full facial alignment and identity preservation. Vertical 9:16 framing. No clothing is visible. Focus tightly on closed eyes, nose, and lips. Face slightly angled to the left side of the frame. Her face is partially submerged in a dark, rich rose-tinted liquid, nearly black beneath the surface, creating cinematic underwater shadowing. Wet black hair flows around the face with vivid neon pink tips reflecting softly in the water. Two hands gently touch each other near the side of her lips, interacting naturally with hair and skin in a neutral editorial manner. Surrounding the face, iridescent bubbles are artfully arranged to frame the face, creating layered depth and compositional interest. A small number of soft soap suds appear around select bubbles for texture. Hair strands float naturally, interacting with bubbles and light.

Mood and Concept:
Cinematic, immersive, and ethereal. Emphasis on editorial composition, layered textures, lighting, and color contrast. Extreme close-up highlights facial structure, bubble framing, and hair movement, with subtle leftward tilt of the face adding dynamic editorial composition.

Makeup and Nails:
Dewy porcelain skin with blush matching neon pink hair tips, applied on cheeks and temples for cohesive color harmony. Eyeshadow in soft pink-violet matching the hair tips, blended smoothly over closed eyelids. Gradient MLBB lips in a subtle rose tone. Fingernails in barely there tint with wet reflective quality.

Hair:
Wet black hair floating around the face with neon pink ends vividly visible and reflecting in the water. Strands interact naturally with bubbles and hands.

Accessories:
None. Only water, bubbles, soap suds, hair, and hands appear in frame.

Photography Specs:
Sony A1 with 90 mm macro lens
Aperture f2.0
Shutter speed 1/200 s
ISO 160
Vertical 9:16 extreme macro with controlled low key lighting and rich color saturation emphasizing underwater depth.

Detail and Finish:
High tactile realism in skin, hair, hands, and bubble membranes. Iridescent thin-film reflections on bubbles and soft soap suds create layered texture. Dark liquid base maintains cinematic shadow depth beneath hair. Neon pink hair tips and matching blush and eyeshadow reflect subtly in water. Wet surfaces preserve natural sheen. Bubbles are arranged to artistically frame the face, enhancing composition and focus. Hands touching near the side of the lips provide compositional balance. Final image reads as a refined, cinematic, editorial high-fashion beauty portrait with closed-eye serenity, subtle leftward angle, and cohesive pink color story.
```

![超写实东亚霓虹夜景人像提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765421937897_vwxh8q_G7k7u74aYAALq9C.jpg)

```
Create a high-resolution vertical 4K photorealistic portrait of him standing on a busy East-Asian street at night. His expression is calm but alert, with subtle reflections of neon lights across his skin. He wears a dark hooded jacket layered under a lightweight streetwear coat.

Motion blur from passing cars, pedestrians, and city lights creates a dynamic sense of movement while the subject remains sharply in focus.

Atmosphere: soft rain mist, drifting steam from a street vent, blurred scooters and cars, neon reflections wrapping around the subject’s shoulders.

Avoid: distorted anatomy, incorrect facial structure (must match reference), double features, overexposure, cartoon/painterly look, text or watermarks, excessive motion blur on the subject.
```

```
{
  "subject": "young woman with long natural black hair and fair skin, wearing a form-fitting, long-sleeved, short-legged deep forest green onesie patterned with small strawberries.",
  "pose": "Standing in profile, facing left, torso slightly turned to glance back at the mirror. Right hand holds a black smartphone to take a selfie. Natural standing posture with relaxed shoulders and a soft, subtle smile.",
  "environment": "Bathroom setting. A white paneled door with silver hardware is directly behind. A white sink basin and chrome faucet occupy the bottom foreground. A white light switch is visible on the left wall.",
  "camera": "Mirror selfie perspective. Shot from chest height, cropping the subject from mid-thigh to just above the head.",
  "lighting": "Standard indoor artificial overhead lighting, casting soft shadows on the door panels and bright reflections on the metallic faucet.",
  "mood_and_expression": "Casual, relaxed selfie posture with a calm and natural expression.",
  "style_and_realism": "Unedited, realistic smartphone photograph.",
  "colors_and_tone": "Warm overall tone dominated by whites, fair skin hues, deep green fabric tones, soft red strawberry accents, and metallic silver/chrome.",
  "quality_and_technical_details": "Typical modern smartphone camera resolution with slight indoor grain and realistic fabric texture.",
  "aspect_ratio_and_output": "3:4",
  "controlnet": {
    "pose_control": {
      "model_type": "openpose_full",
      "purpose": "Preserve exact skeletal alignment, torso orientation, and anatomical proportions without altering mass distribution",
      "constraints": "No limb length change, no torso compression, no posture exaggeration, no anatomical distortion",
      "recommended_weight": 1.1
    },
    "depth_control": {
      "model_type": "depth_midas",
      "purpose": "Preserve accurate 3D spatial depth, volumetric projection, and foreground-background separation",
      "constraints": "No depth flattening, no volumetric distortion, no perspective alteration",
      "recommended_weight": 1.15
    }
  },
  "negative_prompt": "stylization, body reshaping, anatomical distortion, exaggerated curves, volume compression, proportion changes, depth flattening, beautification filters, symmetry correction, perspective alteration, explicit content"
}
```

```
2×2 grid lifestyle collage with a clean fitness and wellness aesthetic, modern social-media style, soft neutral tones.

Top Left Panel – Workout Essentials, ar 5:8

A sensual, blond, beautiful adult woman taking a mirror selfie in a modern kitchen or apartment. She wears a white tank top with deep neckline and light gray fitted shorts, athletic and toned physique. One hand holds a drink, the other holds the phone. Natural daylight, casual confident posture, wellness lifestyle aesthetic.

Bottom Left Panel – Healthy Breakfast Bowl 3:8

Overhead shot of a healthy yogurt bowl arranged neatly with sliced strawberries, blueberries, banana slices, granola, and pink yogurt base. Bright, fresh colors, clean presentation, soft natural light. Emphasis on nutrition and balance.

Bottom Right Panel – Hydration Tracker 2:8

Close-up of a clear reusable water bottle with time markers printed on the side, held by a woman’s hand. Minimal background, clean composition. Highlights hydration, routine, and self-care.

All four images feel cohesive through neutral tones, natural light, minimalist styling, and a calm wellness-focused mood.

Instagram lifestyle aesthetic
Clean and minimal
Wellness and fitness inspired
Soft natural lighting
High realism
```
